        // Store comments in memory
        const comments = [];

        // Function to add a comment
        function addComment() {
            const name = document.getElementById('name').value.trim();
            const comment = document.getElementById('comment').value.trim();

            if (!name || !comment) {
                alert("Please provide both name and comment.");
                return;
            }

            const commentObject = { name, comment };
            comments.push(commentObject);
            displayComments();
            clearInputFields();
        }

        // Function to display comments
        function displayComments() {
            const commentsContainer = document.getElementById('commentsContainer');
            commentsContainer.innerHTML = '';

            comments.forEach((comment, index) => {
                const commentDiv = document.createElement('div');
                commentDiv.className = 'comment';
                commentDiv.innerHTML = `
                    <strong>${comment.name}</strong>
                    <p>${comment.comment}</p>
                    <button onclick="deleteComment(${index})">Delete</button>
                `;
                commentsContainer.appendChild(commentDiv);
            });
        }

        // Function to delete a comment
        function deleteComment(index) {
            comments.splice(index, 1);
            displayComments();
        }

        // Function to clear input fields
        function clearInputFields() {
            document.getElementById('name').value = '';
            document.getElementById('comment').value = '';
        }

        // Function to navigate to the log page
        function goToLogPage() {
            // Store comments in session storage for the log page
            sessionStorage.setItem('comments', JSON.stringify(comments));
            window.location.href = 'log.html';
        }

        // Handle file upload form submission
        document.getElementById('uploadForm').addEventListener('submit', function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            const formData = new FormData(this);
            fetch('/upload', {
                method: 'POST',
                body: formData
            })
            .then(response => response.text())
            .then(data => {
                alert("File uploaded successfully!");
                console.log(data);
            })
            .catch(error => {
                alert("Error uploading file.");
                console.error(error);
            });
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html> -->

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
  <meta charset="UTF-8" />
  <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0"/>
  <title>Main Page</title>
  <style>
    body {
      font-family: Arial, sans-serif;
      margin: 20px;
      line-height: 1.6;
    }
    .comment-section {
      margin-top: 20px;
    }
    .comment {
      border: 1px solid #ccc;
      padding: 10px;
      margin-bottom: 10px;
      border-radius: 5px;
    }
    .comment button {
      margin-top: 10px;
      padding: 5px 10px;
    }
  </style>
</head>
<body>
  <h1>Welcome to the Main Page</h1>
  <div>
    <label for="name">Name:</label>
    <input type="text" id="name" placeholder="Enter your name" />
  </div>
  <div>
    <label for="comment">Comment:</label>
    <textarea id="comment" placeholder="Leave a comment"></textarea>
  </div>
  <button onclick="addComment()">Submit Comment</button>
  <h2>Upload File (Chunked)</h2>
  <!--
       We keep a "form-like" structure for user convenience, but we will NOT use
       the default submit. Instead, we'll handle the chunked upload via JavaScript.
  -->
  <div>
    <input type="file" id="fileInput" name="file" />
    <button onclick="uploadFileChunked()">Upload in Chunks</button>
  </div>
  <!-- Progress/Status area (optional) -->
  <div id="uploadStatus"></div>
  <h2>Comments</h2>
  <div id="commentsContainer" class="comment-section"></div>
  <button onclick="goToLogPage()">Go to Log Page</button>
  <script>
    // ------------------------------
    //   COMMENT FUNCTIONS
    // ------------------------------
    const comments = [];
    function addComment() {
      const name = document.getElementById('name').value.trim();
      const comment = document.getElementById('comment').value.trim();
      if (!name || !comment) {
        alert("Please provide both name and comment.");
        return;
      }
      const commentObject = { name, comment };
      comments.push(commentObject);
      displayComments();
      clearInputFields();
    }
    function displayComments() {
      const commentsContainer = document.getElementById('commentsContainer');
      commentsContainer.innerHTML = '';
      comments.forEach((comment, index) => {
        const commentDiv = document.createElement('div');
        commentDiv.className = 'comment';
        commentDiv.innerHTML = `
          <strong>${comment.name}</strong>
          <p>${comment.comment}</p>
          <button onclick="deleteComment(${index})">Delete</button>
        `;
        commentsContainer.appendChild(commentDiv);
      });
    }
    function deleteComment(index) {
      comments.splice(index, 1);
      displayComments();
    }
    function clearInputFields() {
      document.getElementById('name').value = '';
      document.getElementById('comment').value = '';
    }
    function goToLogPage() {
      // Store comments in session storage for the log page
      sessionStorage.setItem('comments', JSON.stringify(comments));
      window.location.href = 'log.html';
    }
    // ------------------------------
    //   CHUNKED UPLOAD FUNCTION
    // ------------------------------
    // Change this endpoint to the actual server route that handles chunked uploads.
    const uploadEndpoint = "/upload-chunk";
    // Adjust this chunk size to suit your needs (e.g., 1MB = 1024*1024)
    const CHUNK_SIZE = 1024 * 512; // 512 KB for demo
    function uploadFileChunked() {
      const fileInput = document.getElementById('fileInput');
      if (!fileInput.files.length) {
        alert("Please select a file before uploading.");
        return;
      }
      const file = fileInput.files[0];
      let offset = 0;
      const totalSize = file.size;
      const statusDiv = document.getElementById('uploadStatus');
      statusDiv.innerHTML = `Uploading "${file.name}" in chunks...`;
      // Read and upload the next chunk:
      function uploadNextChunk() {
        const chunk = file.slice(offset, offset + CHUNK_SIZE);
        const reader = new FileReader();
        reader.onload = async function(e) {
          try {
            const chunkData = e.target.result; // ArrayBuffer
            // Prepare form data
            const formData = new FormData();
            // We'll include chunk number, file name, etc.
            formData.append('fileChunk', new Blob([chunkData]), file.name);
            formData.append('chunkStart', offset);
            formData.append('chunkEnd', offset + CHUNK_SIZE);
            formData.append('totalSize', totalSize);
            formData.append('fileName', file.name);
            // Send the chunk to the server
            const response = await fetch(uploadEndpoint, {
              method: "POST",
              body: formData
            });
            if (!response.ok) {
              throw new Error(`Server error: ${response.statusText}`);
            }
            // Move on to the next chunk
            offset += CHUNK_SIZE;
            const percent = Math.min(((offset / totalSize) * 100).toFixed(2), 100);
            statusDiv.innerHTML = `Uploading "${file.name}"... ${percent}%`;
            // If there's still more file left, continue uploading
            if (offset < totalSize) {
              uploadNextChunk();
            } else {
              statusDiv.innerHTML = `Upload complete for "${file.name}"!`;
            }
          } catch (error) {
            console.error("Chunk upload error:", error);
            statusDiv.innerHTML = `Error uploading file: ${error.message}`;
          }
        };
        // Read the chunk as an ArrayBuffer
        reader.readAsArrayBuffer(chunk);
      }
      // Start the upload
      uploadNextChunk();
    }
  </script>
</body>
</html>
